<p style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><strong><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</i></strong></p>

<p style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><strong><span style="font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:
&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast">Classification of
Steels :</span></strong><i><span style="font-size:10.0pt">&nbsp;mild steal &amp; alloy steel, Heat treatment of
steel, Welding – Arc Welding, Gas Welding, Resistance Welding, Special Welding
Techniques i.e. TIG, MIG, etc. (Brazing &amp; Soldering), Welding Defects &amp;
Testing; NDT, Foundry &amp; Casting – methods, defects, different casting
processes, Forging, Extrusion, etc, Metal cutting principles, cutting tools,
Basic Principles of machining with (i) Lathe (ii) Milling (iii) Drilling (iv)
Shaping (v) Grinding, Machines, tools &amp; manufacturing processes.</span></i></span></p>

<p style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><i style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</i></p>

<p style="margin: 0in 0in 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><br></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Railway is one of those institutions that people wish to work with.
Every year Railway Recruitment Board conducts exams for the recruitment of
candidates at various posts under the non-technical and technical categories.</span></i></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">The technical exams are carried out by the different RRBs in different
states. There are 5 exams that RRB conducts, these a</span></i></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">1) RRB ALP</span></i></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">2) RRB JE/SSE</span></i></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">3) RRC Group D</span></i></p>

<p class="uiqtextpara" style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
margin-left:0in"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">4) RRB NTPC</span></i></p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;">Further
RRB <span style="background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">is planning to recruit&nbsp;</span></span></i><strong><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">5620 engineer</span></strong><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">&nbsp;soon by this
year . For this, only candidates having 3 years diploma in Engineering will be
invited to submit online application.</span></i></span></p>

<div style="border-top: none; border-right: none; border-left: none; border-image: initial; border-bottom: 1pt solid windowtext; padding: 0in 0in 1pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;">

<span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><h3 style="margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:8.5pt;margin-left:
0in;background:white;border:none;mso-border-bottom-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
padding:0in;mso-padding-alt:0in 0in 1.0pt 0in"><i><span style="font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-weight:normal">Indicative
Syllabus</span></i></h3>

</span></div>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">The standard of the questions in
Engineering subjects will be approximately of the level of Diploma in
Engineering from a recognized Institute, Board or University recognized by All
India Board of Technical Education.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">General
Intelligence and Reasoning Syllabus</span></i></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Number
Series, Input-Output, syllogism, Coding-decoding.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Word
Building, Clock, Seating arrangement, Calendar.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Decision
making, Direction sense test, visual memory, Blood relations, figural
classification and arithmetical reasoning.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Similarities
and differences, space visualization /orientation, analogy.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Coding
&amp; Decoding, Arithmetic number series, non-verbal series, Statement
conclusion</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">General
Awareness Syllabus</span></i></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">General
Awareness on Railway.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">New
Technologies &amp; Reform in Indian Railway.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Rail
Budget.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Indian –
History, Geography, Polity, Economy Current Affairs, Sports, etc</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Arithmetic
Syllabus</span></i></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Algebra.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Ratio
&amp; Proportion.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Interests.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">percentage</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Profit
&amp; loss.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Time and
distance /work.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Pipes
&amp; Cisterns.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Age
problems.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Mensuration.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Data
Interpretation.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><strong><span style="font-size: 10pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Technical Syllabus Tentative: </span></strong></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Electronics
Engineering Syllabus</span></i></b></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Electronic
Devices.</span></i></span></p>

/Digital Electronics.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Circuits.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Industrial
Instrumentation.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Process

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Civil

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Estimating.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Costing.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">General
Civil Engineering.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Construction
/Structure Engineering and drawing.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Valuation.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Structural

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Building

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Mechanics.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Concrete

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Steel

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Construction.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Hydraulics.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Highway

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Traffic

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Projections.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Environmental

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Surveying.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Coordinate

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">curves.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Measurements

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 13pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><b><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">IT

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;MS

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Information

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Computer

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">C , C++

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">DBMS.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Software

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">System

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">SAD.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">UNIX.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Web

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Data &amp;

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Operating
systems.</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 46.5pt; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp; </span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Environment
&amp; Pollution Control</span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 28.5pt; line-height: 13pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">The Delhi Metro has been instrumental in ushering in a new

<ul type="disc"><li>
 </li><li class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><i><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;">Figures Classification.</span></i></li><li>

</span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Test of direction sense </span></i></span></p>

<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.25in; line-height: 12pt; background-image: initial; background-position: initial; background-size: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="font-size: 10pt;">·<span style="font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; font-stretch: normal; font-size: 7pt; line-height: normal;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><!--[endif]--><i><span style="font-size: 10pt;">Arithmetical Reasoning </span></i></span></p>
